9th - 32nd Decklists
====================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 28, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











In a tournament over 2800 players, there might have been a few near misses and we didn't want you to miss out on the top finishing decks of the weekend. Most of these players were one match win or even one match point away from the Top 8! Let's check them out!







#### Kenta Masukado's 4-Color Company


##### 
 Grand Prix Kobe 2017, 9th Place






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
